As an old five-star hotel, it's really not satisfactory

I especially want to complain about breakfast. I went downstairs at 9:30 and was told to collect the meal immediately. If I take more, it will be gone later. There is no air conditioner on the breakfast floor. It is not an exaggeration to go to the room to take a shower after breakfast. Are five-star hotels reluctant to turn on the air conditioner? I won't choose this hotel next time, let's go to Hilton
